A complex sentence   has a main  clause and one   or more adverbial clauses   Adverbial clauses usually come   after the   main   clause
We  were proud that  you conc  eded defeat so graciously.Does the part you conceded defeat so graciously fall under independent, infinitive, surbodinating or   co-ordinating  clause?
